SELECT FKTRA_NPER_NCODIGO, COUNT(*) AS CANTIDAD FROM u632406828_dbp_whatsappbo.tbl_ctransferencias, u632406828_dbp_whatsappbo.tbl_rpermiso WHERE PKPER_NCODIGO = FKTRA_NPER_NCODIGO AND TRA_CFECHA_REGISTRO BETWEEN '2021-12-28 00:00:00' AND '2021-12-28 23:59:59' AND TRA_CESTADO = 'Activo' GROUP BY FKTRA_NPER_NCODIGO ORDER BY CANTIDAD ASC;
